(function () {
  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch &amp;&amp; sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  };

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj &amp;&amp; typeof (obj) === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function (k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  };

  function getAppName() {
    return get('_wml.config.ui.applicationName', window);
  }

  function getMidasConfig() {
    return get('_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig', window) || {};
  };
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get('_wml.config.ui.midasConfig', window) || {};
  };
  
  function getMidasCfgVal(cfgName) {
    var cfg = getMidasConfig();
    var appName = getAppName();
    var pageCfgKey = appName + '-' + cfgName;
    return cfg[pageCfgKey] || cfg[cfgName];
  }

  function loadScript(scriptUrl) {
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  };

  function loadAds() {
    if (!loadAds.loaded) {
      var hasPerfMark = !!get('performance.mark', window);
      if (hasPerfMark) {
        // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
        window.performance.mark('load-midas-display');
      }
      loadAds.loaded = true;
      var displayAds = (getMidasCfgVal("displayAds") !== "false");
      if (displayAds) {
        var MDABT = getCookie("MDABT");
        var midasDisplayScript = getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABT) || getMidasCfgVal("midasDisplayScript");
        var gptUrl = "//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js";
        loadScript(midasDisplayScript);
        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  };

  function loadS2SScripts() {
    if (!loadS2SScripts.loaded) {
      var hasPerfMark = !!get('performance.mark', window);
      if (hasPerfMark) {
        // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
        window.performance.mark('load-s2s-midas-scripts');
      }
      loadS2SScripts.loaded = true;
      var MDABTS2S = getCookie("MDABTS2S");
      var midasS2SScript = getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABTS2S) || getMidasCfgVal("midasS2SScript");
      loadScript(midasS2SScript);
    }
  }

  var loadS2SEvent = (
    getCookie('loadS2SEvent') ||
    getMidasUiConfig()['loadS2SEvent'] ||
    getMidasCfgVal('loadS2SEvent') ||
    'hasS2SPayload'
  );

  var loadEvent = (
    getCookie('loadEvent') ||
    getMidasUiConfig()['loadEvent'] ||
    getMidasCfgVal('loadEvent') ||
    'instant'
  );
  window._wml.adLoader = function () {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function (listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      }
    };
  }();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent('instant'); // Default load ads immediately
})();
  </script>

               <div class="ExpandableHtmlText">

                 <div class="collapsable has-toggle" id="Collapsable-1586032979216" style="min-height: 100px;">
                  <div class="collapsable-content-container">
                   <div>
                    <div class="ExpandableHtmlText-markup">
                     <h2>
                      Cleaning Supplies
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      Keeping a clean home doesn't have to be as arduous or expensive as you may think. With the right supplies, you can work smarter rather than harder to keep your home looking clean and smelling fresh.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      Begin by taking an inventory of the supplies that you have on hand, then create a shopping list and pick up what's missing. Most essential cleaning supplies fall into three main categories: picker-uppers, brushes and
                      <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/home-improvement/brooms/1072864_1230393_1231141" tabindex="-1">
                       brooms
                      </a>
                      , and cleaning solutions.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      Picker-uppers include
                      <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/office/paper/1229749_6562796" tabindex="-1">
                       paper
                      </a>
                      -towels'&gt;paper towels, non-abrasive scrubbing pads, reusable cleaning wipes and sponges. Essential brushes and brooms include a broom and dust pan, toilet brushes (one to keep by each toilet) and a scrub brush. You may also want to consider specialty brushes such as a vent brush, a window blind brush or a
                      <a href="https://www.walmart.com/browse/home-improvement/ceiling-fans/1072864_133032_5294047" tabindex="-1">
                       ceiling fan
                      </a>
                      brush for particularly difficult jobs. Crucial cleaning solutions include all-purpose spray cleaner, window cleaner, toilet bowl cleaner, bleach, hard-water mineral remover, enzymatic carpet cleaner (if you have carpeting), tile and grout cleaning solution and metal polish. You can save money by buying economy size cleaners and using refillable spray bottles.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      With a huge selection of cleaning supplies at Everyday Low Prices, Walmart has you covered. Save money. Live better.
                     </p>
                    </div>
